User instruction received\n2. Diff generated and surfaced\n3. User approved the change\n4. Change applied to artifact\n5. Hot-reload verified (no redeploy needed)\n\n## Deliverables Completed\n\n### 1. Self-Modification Agent\n**File:** `src/agents/self_modification.py`\n\nCapabilities:\n- Reads artifacts (prompts, configs) from disk\n- Generates diffs based on user instructions\n- Surfaces changes for approval with confidence scores\n- Applies approved changes to disk\n- Supports rollback via git history or component versioning\n\n### 2. Component Library\n**Files:** `src/components/library.py`, `data/schema.sql`\n\nTables:\n- `components` - Current component versions\n- `component_versions` - Version history\n- `card_cache` - Rendered card cache\n- `component_usage_patterns` - Historical matching data\n\nCapabilities:\n- Create/update components with versioning\n- Find best-fit components by semantic match\n- Cache rendered cards\n- Track usage patterns for future matching\n\n### 3. UI-Regen Agent\n**File:** `src/agents/ui_regen.py`\n\nCapabilities:\n- Finds best-fit component for result data\n- Generates new components from result shapes\n- Applies templates to result data\n- Iterates components based on user feedback\n\n### 4. Hot-Reload Manager\n**File:** `src/components/hot_reload.py`\n\nMonitored artifacts:\n- `prompts/router.md`\n- `prompts/synthesize.md`\n- `prompts/voice.md`\n- `prompts/urgency.md`\n- `prompts/fetch/status.md`\n- `prompts/fetch/action.md`\n- `config/registry.yaml`\n- `config/monitoring.yaml`\n- `config/exceptions.yaml`\n\nCapabilities:\n- Per-invocation mtime checking\n- Automatic reload when files change\n- Force reload API\n\n### 5. SSE Component Updates\n**File:** `src/sse/events.py`\n\nEvent types:\n- `component_updated` - Broadcasts component version changes\n\nCanvas re-renders affected cards when component version changes.\n\n### 6. Feedback Processor\n**File:** `src/feedback/processor.py`\n\nWorkflow:\n1. Receives user feedback instruction\n2. Identifies target artifact\n3. Generates diff via self-modification agent\n4. Surfaces for approval (if required)\n5. Applies or rejects based on user decision\n6. Broadcasts update via SSE\n\n### 7. API Endpoints\n**File:** `src/main.py`\n\nEndpoints:\n- `POST /api/v1/feedback` - Process feedback\n- `POST /api/v1/feedback/approve` - Approve change\n- `POST /api/v1/feedback/reject` - Reject change\n- `GET /api/v1/feedback/pending` - List pending approvals\n- `POST /api/v1/feedback/rollback` - Rollback artifact\n- `GET /api/v1/components` - List components\n- `POST /api/v1/components` - Create component\n- `POST /api/v1/components/{id}` - Update component\n- `POST /api/v1/components/{id}/iterate` - Iterate component\n- `GET /api/v1/components/{id}/history` - Component history\n\n## Test Coverage\n\n**File:** `test_phase2.py`\n\nAll tests passing:\n- Self-modification cycle test\n- Component library test\n- UI-regen agent test\n- Feedback processor test\n- SSE component updates test\n\n## Demo\n\n**File:** `demo_self_modification.py`\n\nDemonstrates complete self-modification cycle with user instruction → diff → approval → application → hot-reload.\n\n## Architecture Notes\n\n1. **Per-invocation reload:** Artifacts are checked for mtime changes on every call. No file watching needed for personal single-user scale.\n\n2. **Safety model:** All changes go through diff review. Rollback available for any artifact via git history (prompts/configs) or version history (components).\n\n3. **Component matching:** Semantic scoring uses keyword matching. In production, this would use embeddings for better matching.\n\n4. **LLM integration:** The `_generate_update` and `_improve_template` methods use simple heuristics for now. For now, use simple keyword match)\n        components = conn.execute(\n            \"SELECT id, name, description FROM components WHERE usage_count > 0\"\n        ).fetchall()\n\n        best_component = None\n        best_score = 0.0\n\n        for comp_id, name, description in components:\n            score = self._semantic_score(result_type, name, description)\n            if score > best_score:\n                best_score = score\n                best_component = self.get_component(comp_id)\n\n        # Only return if we have reasonable confidence\n        if best_score >= 0.5:\n            return best_component\n\n        return None\n\n    def _semantic_score(self, result_type: str, comp_name: str, comp_description: str) -> float:\n        \"\"\"\n        Calculate semantic match score.\n\n        Simple keyword-based scoring. In production, use embeddings.\n        \"\"\"\n        result_type_lower = result_type.lower()\n        comp_name_lower = comp_name.lower()\n        comp_desc_lower = comp_description.lower()\n\n        score = 0.0\n\n        # Exact name match\n        if result_type_lower == comp_name_lower:\n            return 1.0\n\n        # Name contains result type\n        if result_type_lower in comp_name_lower:\n            score += 0.7\n\n        # Description contains keywords from result type\n        result_keywords = result_type_lower.replace('-', ' ').split()\n        for keyword in result_keywords:\n            if keyword in comp_desc_lower:\n                score += 0.1\n\n        return min(score, 1.0)\n\n    def update_component(\n        self,\n        component_id: str,\n        html_template: str,\n        change_note: str\n    ) -> Optional[Component]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Update a component to a new version.\n\n        Invalidates all cached cards using this component.\n\n        Args:\n            component_id: The component to update\n            html_template: The new template\n            change_note: Why this change was made\n\n        Returns:\n            The updated Component, or None if not found\n        \"\"\"\n        conn = self._get_conn()\n\n        # Get current version\n        row = conn.execute(\n            \"SELECT version FROM components WHERE id = ?\",\n            (component_id,)\n        ).fetchone()\n\n        if not row:\n            return None\n\n        new_version = row[0] + 1\n        now = int(time.time())\n\n        # Update component\n        conn.execute(\n            \"\"\"\n            UPDATE components\n            SET html_template = ?, version = ?, last_used = ?\n            WHERE id = ?\n            \"\"\",\n            (html_template, new_version, now, component_id)\n        )\n\n        # Add version history\n        conn.execute(\n            \"\"\"\n            INSERT INTO component_versions (component_id, version, html_template, created_at, change_note)\n            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n            \"\"\",\n            (component_id, new_version, html_template, now, change_note)\n        )\n\n        # Update component usage stats\n        conn.execute(\n            \"\"\"\n            UPDATE components\n            SET usage_count = usage_count + 1, last_used = ?\n            WHERE id = ?\n            \"\"\",\n            (int(time.time()), component_id)\n        )\n        conn.commit()\n\n    def get_cached_card(\n        self,\n        result_id: str,\n        component_id: str,\n        layout_bucket: str\n    ) -> Optional[CachedCard]:\n        \"\"\"Get a cached card if it exists and is up-to-date.\"\"\"\n        conn = self._get_conn()\n        row = conn.execute(\n            \"\"\"\n            SELECT result_id, component_id, component_version, layout_bucket, rendered_html, created_at\n            FROM card_cache\n            WHERE result_id = ?   self,\n        component_id: str,\n        result_type: str,\n        match_score: float\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Record a component usage pattern for future matching.\n\n        Args:\n            component_id: The component that was used\n            result_type: The type of result it rendered\n            match_score: How well it matched (0-1)\n        \"\"\"\n        conn = self._get_conn()\n        now = int(time.time())\n\n        conn.execute(\n            \"\"\"\n            INSERT INTO component_usage_patterns (component_id, result_type, match_score, sample_count,
